    \def\doxynewunicodechar#1#2{%
    \@tempswafalse
    \edef\nuc@tempa{\detokenize{#1}}%
    \if\relax\nuc@tempa\relax
      \nuc@emptyargerr
    \else
      \edef\@tempb{\expandafter\@car\nuc@tempa\@nil}%
      \nuc@check
      \if@tempswa
        \@namedef{u8:\nuc@tempa}{#2}%
      \fi
    \fi
  }
